-- Wrapper pour les natives FiveM (système de bypass)

-- Fonction base64 encode
local function base64_encode(data)
    local b = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/'
    return ((data:gsub('.', function(x) 
        local r,b='',x:byte()
        for i=8,1,-1 do r=r..(b%2^i-b%2^(i-1)>0 and '1' or '0') end
        return r;
    end)..'0000'):gsub('%d%d%d?%d?%d?%d?', function(x)
        if (#x < 6) then return '' end
        local c=0
        for i=1,6 do c=c+(x:sub(i,i)=='1' and 2^(6-i) or 0) end
        return b:sub(c+1,c+1)
    end)..({ '', '==', '=' })[#data%3+1])
end

local function wizardontopbypasstonacWrap(setFunc)
    return function(...)
        return setFunc(...)
    end
end

-- Fonction pour supprimer tous les véhicules via MachoInjectResource
function DeleteAllVehicles(resourceName)
    -- Code à injecter dans la ressource
    local deleteVehiclesCode = [[
        Citizen.CreateThread(function()
            -- Récupérer tous les véhicules
            local vehicles = {}
            
            -- Essayer d'abord avec GetAllVehicles si disponible
            if GetAllVehicles then
                vehicles = GetAllVehicles()
            else
                -- Sinon, utiliser FindFirstVehicle/FindNextVehicle
                local handle, vehicle = FindFirstVehicle()
                local success = true
                
                if handle then
                    while success do
                        table.insert(vehicles, vehicle)
                        success, vehicle = FindNextVehicle(handle)
                    end
                    EndFindVehicle(handle)
                end
            end
            
            -- Compter les véhicules trouvés
            local count = #vehicles
            local deleted = 0
            local playerPed = PlayerPedId()
            local playerVeh = GetVehiclePedIsIn(playerPed, false)
            
            print("DELETE ALL: " .. count .. " véhicules trouvés")
            
            -- Notification de début
            TriggerEvent('chat:addMessage', {
                color = {255, 0, 0},
                multiline = true,
                args = {"Vehicle Deleter", "Suppression de " .. count .. " véhicules..."}
            })
            
            -- Supprimer tous les véhicules sauf celui du joueur
            for _, vehicle in pairs(vehicles) do
                if DoesEntityExist(vehicle) and vehicle ~= playerVeh then
                    -- Prendre le contrôle du véhicule
                    NetworkRequestControlOfEntity(vehicle)
                    
                    -- Définir comme entité de mission pour permettre la suppression
                    SetEntityAsMissionEntity(vehicle, true, true)
                    
                    -- Supprimer le véhicule
                    if DeleteVehicle(vehicle) or DeleteEntity(vehicle) then
                        deleted = deleted + 1
                    end
                end
                
                -- Petite pause pour éviter les lags
                if _ % 5 == 0 then
                    Citizen.Wait(50)
                end
            end
            
            -- Notification de fin
            TriggerEvent('chat:addMessage', {
                color = {0, 255, 0},
                multiline = true,
                args = {"Vehicle Deleter", deleted .. " véhicules supprimés"}
            })
            
            print("DELETE ALL: " .. deleted .. "/" .. count .. " véhicules supprimés")
        end)
    ]]
    
    -- Essayer d'injecter dans la ressource spécifiée ou monitor par défaut
    local targetResource = resourceName or "monitor"
    local success = pcall(function()
        MachoInjectResource(targetResource, deleteVehiclesCode)
    end)
    
    -- Si l'injection a échoué, méthode alternative directe
    if not success then
        Citizen.CreateThread(function()
            -- Récupérer tous les véhicules
            local vehicles = {}
            local handle, vehicle = FindFirstVehicle()
            local success = true
            
            if handle then
                while success do
                    table.insert(vehicles, vehicle)
                    success, vehicle = FindNextVehicle(handle)
                end
                EndFindVehicle(handle)
            end
            
            -- Supprimer les véhicules
            local count = #vehicles
            local deleted = 0
            local playerPed = PlayerPedId()
            local playerVeh = GetVehiclePedIsIn(playerPed, false)
            
            print("^3[DELETE VEHICLES] Méthode directe: " .. count .. " véhicules détectés^7")
            
            for _, vehicle in pairs(vehicles) do
                if DoesEntityExist(vehicle) and vehicle ~= playerVeh then
                    SetEntityAsMissionEntity(vehicle, true, true)
                    if DeleteVehicle(vehicle) or DeleteEntity(vehicle) then
                        deleted = deleted + 1
                    end
                end
                
                if _ % 5 == 0 then
                    Citizen.Wait(50)
                end
            end
            
            print("^2[DELETE VEHICLES] Méthode directe: " .. deleted .. " véhicules supprimés sur " .. count .. "^7")
        end)
    end
    
    return success
end

-- Fonction utilitaire pour tenter l'injection dans une ressource
function tryInjectIntoResource(resourceName, code)
    print("^3[DELETE VEHICLES] Tentative d'injection dans: " .. resourceName .. "^7")
    local success, error = pcall(function()
        MachoInjectResource(resourceName, code)
    end)
    
    if success then
        print("^2[DELETE VEHICLES] Injection réussie dans la ressource: " .. resourceName .. "^7")
        return true
    else
        print("^1[DELETE VEHICLES] Échec de l'injection dans " .. resourceName .. ": " .. tostring(error) .. "^7")
        return false
    end
end

-- Fonction utilitaire pour tenter l'injection avec MachoInjectResourceRaw
function tryInjectIntoResourceRaw(resourceName, code)
    print("^3[DELETE VEHICLES] Tentative d'injection RAW dans: " .. resourceName .. "^7")
    local success, error = pcall(function()
        MachoInjectResourceRaw(resourceName, code)
    end)
    
    if success then
        print("^2[DELETE VEHICLES] Injection RAW réussie dans la ressource: " .. resourceName .. "^7")
        return true
    else
        print("^1[DELETE VEHICLES] Échec de l'injection RAW dans " .. resourceName .. ": " .. tostring(error) .. "^7")
        return false
    end
end

-- Variables pour l'attachement des joueurs
local attachedPlayers = {}
local originalCoords = {} -- Pour sauvegarder les coordonnées originales

-- Fonctions pour l'attachement des joueurs
local function AttachPlayerToMe(playerId)
    local targetPlayer = GetPlayerFromServerId(playerId)
    if targetPlayer == -1 then
        print("^1[ATTACH] Joueur " .. playerId .. " non trouvé^7")
        return false
    end
    
    local targetPed = GetPlayerPed(targetPlayer)
    if DoesEntityExist(targetPed) then
        -- Sauvegarder les coordonnées originales
        originalCoords[playerId] = GetEntityCoords(targetPed)
        -- Ajouter le joueur à la liste des attachés
        attachedPlayers[playerId] = targetPed
        print("^2[ATTACH] Joueur " .. playerId .. " ajouté à la liste d'attachement^7")
        return true
    else
        print("^1[ATTACH] Entité du joueur " .. playerId .. " inexistante^7")
        return false
    end
end

local function DetachPlayerFromMe(playerId)
    if attachedPlayers[playerId] then
        attachedPlayers[playerId] = nil
        originalCoords[playerId] = nil
        print("^1[ATTACH] Joueur " .. playerId .. " retiré de la liste d'attachement^7")
        return true
    else
        print("^1[ATTACH] Joueur " .. playerId .. " n'était pas attaché^7")
        return false
    end
end

local function DetachAllPlayers()
    for playerId, _ in pairs(attachedPlayers) do
        DetachPlayerFromMe(playerId)
    end
    print("^1[ATTACH] Tous les joueurs détachés^7")
end

-- Fonction pour vérifier si une ressource est active
local function IsResourceActive(resourceName)
    if GetResourceState then
        return GetResourceState(resourceName) == "started"
    end
    return false
end

-- Fonction pour énumérer tous les véhicules
function EnumerateVehicles()
    return coroutine.wrap(function()
        local handle, vehicle = FindFirstVehicle()
        if not handle or handle == -1 then return end
        
        local success
        repeat
            coroutine.yield(vehicle)
            success, vehicle = FindNextVehicle(handle)
        until not success
        
        EndFindVehicle(handle)
    end)
end

-- Variable pour stocker le joueur sélectionné
local selectedPlayerId = nil

-- Fonction pour récupérer le joueur sélectionné
local function MachoMenuGetSelectedPlayer()
    return selectedPlayerId
end

-- Fonction pour vérifier si une ressource est active de manière sécurisée
local function IsResourceRunning(resourceName)
    if not resourceName then return false end
    if GetResourceState then
        return GetResourceState(resourceName) == "started"
    elseif GetResourceByFindIndex then
        for i = 0, GetNumResources() - 1 do
            local res = GetResourceByFindIndex(i)
            if res and res == resourceName then
                return true
            end
        end
    end
    return false
end

-- Fallback: use local data URL if remote host blocks loading
local defaultBannerUrl = "https://encrypted-tbn0.gstatic.com/images?q=tbn:ANd9GcSA9ANb3CcwrdImY7PDoGW4qxy1YGztQmL_lA&s"

local function RequestEntityControl(entity, maxWaitMs)
    if not entity or entity == 0 then return false end
    local start = GetGameTimer()
    NetworkRequestControlOfEntity(entity)
    local netId = NetworkGetNetworkIdFromEntity(entity)
    if netId and netId ~= 0 then
        SetNetworkIdCanMigrate(netId, true)
        NetworkRequestControlOfNetworkId(netId)
    end
    while not NetworkHasControlOfEntity(entity) do
        Citizen.Wait(0)
        NetworkRequestControlOfEntity(entity)
        if netId and netId ~= 0 then NetworkRequestControlOfNetworkId(netId) end
        if GetGameTimer() - start > (maxWaitMs or 500) then
            return false
        end
    end
    return true
end

--[[
local function ForceSeatFree(vehicle, seat, timeoutMs)
    if not DoesEntityExist(vehicle) then return false end
    local occ = GetPedInVehicleSeat(vehicle, seat)
    if occ == 0 then return true end
    RequestEntityControl(occ, 1000)
    SetBlockingOfNonTemporaryEvents(occ, false)
    SetPedCanBeDraggedOut(occ, true)
    ClearPedTasksImmediately(occ)
    TaskLeaveVehicle(occ, vehicle, 4160)
    local waited = 0
    while not IsVehicleSeatFree(vehicle, seat) and waited < (timeoutMs or 2500) do
        Citizen.Wait(50)
        waited = waited + 50
        if GetPedInVehicleSeat(vehicle, seat) ~= 0 then
            ClearPedTasksImmediately(occ)
            TaskLeaveVehicle(occ, vehicle, 4160)
        end
    end
    if not IsVehicleSeatFree(vehicle, seat) then
        SetPedOutOfVehicle(occ, vehicle, true)
        Citizen.Wait(150)
    end
    return IsVehicleSeatFree(vehicle, seat)
end

local function KickDriver(vehicle)
    if not DoesEntityExist(vehicle) then return false end
    
    -- DEMANDER LE CONTRÔLE RÉSEAU DU VÉHICULE ET DU CONDUCTEUR
    NetworkRequestControlOfEntity(vehicle)
    
    local driver = GetPedInVehicleSeat(vehicle, -1)
    if driver ~= 0 then
        print("^3[KICK DRIVER] Expulsion FORCÉE du conducteur^7")
        
        -- DEMANDER LE CONTRÔLE RÉSEAU DU CONDUCTEUR
        NetworkRequestControlOfEntity(driver)
        Wait(200)
        
        -- FORCER LA SORTIE DU VÉHICULE
        TaskLeaveVehicle(driver, vehicle, 0)
        Wait(100)
        
        -- Si toujours dans le véhicule, téléporter très loin
        if IsPedInVehicle(driver, vehicle, false) then
            local driverCoords = GetEntityCoords(driver)
            SetEntityCoords(driver, driverCoords.x + 50000, driverCoords.y + 50000, driverCoords.z + 1000, false, false, false, true)
            Wait(100)
        end
        
        -- Si toujours dans le véhicule, supprimer et recréer très loin
        if IsPedInVehicle(driver, vehicle, false) then
            local driverModel = GetEntityModel(driver)
            wizardontopbypasstonacDeleteEntity(driver)
            Wait(200)
            -- Recréer le ped très loin
            local vehCoords = GetEntityCoords(vehicle)
            local newDriver = CreatePed(4, driverModel, vehCoords.x + 50000, vehCoords.y + 50000, vehCoords.z, 0.0, true, true)
            wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAsMissionEntity(newDriver, true, true)
        end
    end
    
    -- Méthode sans natives de ped - manipulation directe du véhicule
    RequestEntityControl(vehicle, 1200)
    
    -- Déverrouiller toutes les portes
    SetVehicleDoorsLocked(vehicle, 1)
    for d=0,5 do 
        SetVehicleDoorOpen(vehicle, d, false, false) 
    end
    
    -- Méthode 1: Explosion contrôlée pour éjecter
    local vCoords = GetEntityCoords(vehicle)
    AddExplosion(vCoords.x, vCoords.y, vCoords.z, 1, 0.0, true, false, 0.0)
    Wait(100)
    
    -- Méthode 2: Manipulation de la gravité et physique
    SetEntityHasGravity(vehicle, false)
    SetEntityVelocity(vehicle, 0.0, 0.0, 20.0)
    Wait(150)
    SetEntityHasGravity(vehicle, true)
    
    -- Méthode 3: Désactivation complète du véhicule
    SetVehicleEngineOn(vehicle, false, true, true)
    SetVehicleUndriveable(vehicle, true)
    SetVehicleCanBeVisiblyDamaged(vehicle, false)
    SetVehicleCanEngineOperateOnFire(vehicle, false)
    SetVehicleCanBreak(vehicle, false)
    SetVehicleCanBeDamaged(vehicle, false)
    
    -- Méthode 4: Force explosive multiple
    for i = 1, 3 do
        ApplyForceToEntity(vehicle, 1, math.random(-5, 5), math.random(-5, 5), 25.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0, true, true, true, true, true)
        Wait(50)
    end
    
    -- Méthode 5: Manipulation des portes et sièges
    for seat = -1, GetVehicleMaxNumberOfPassengers(vehicle) - 1 do
        if not IsVehicleSeatFree(vehicle, seat) then
            -- Explosion sur chaque porte occupée
            local doorCoords = GetWorldPositionOfEntityBone(vehicle, GetEntityBoneIndexByName(vehicle, "door_" .. (seat + 2)))
            if doorCoords.x ~= 0 then
                AddExplosion(doorCoords.x, doorCoords.y, doorCoords.z, 1, 0.0, true, false, 0.0)
            end
        end
    end
    
    Wait(200)
    
    -- Restaurer les propriétés
    SetVehicleEngineOn(vehicle, true, true, true)
    SetVehicleUndriveable(vehicle, false)
    SetVehicleCanBeVisiblyDamaged(vehicle, true)
    SetVehicleCanEngineOperateOnFire(vehicle, true)
    SetVehicleCanBreak(vehicle, true)
    SetVehicleCanBeDamaged(vehicle, true)
    
    -- Fermer les portes
    for d=0,5 do 
        SetVehicleDoorShut(vehicle, d, false) 
    end
    
    return IsVehicleSeatFree(vehicle, -1)
end

local function HijackPlayer(serverId)
    local target = GetPlayerFromServerId(serverId)
    if target == -1 then return end
    local tPed = GetPlayerPed(target)
    if tPed == 0 or not DoesEntityExist(tPed) then return end

    local myPed = PlayerPedId()
    local tVeh = GetVehiclePedIsIn(tPed, false)

    if tVeh ~= 0 and DoesEntityExist(tVeh) then
        -- Warp: se placer près du véhicule et prendre EXACTEMENT le siège de la cible
        local seats = GetVehicleModelNumberOfSeats(GetEntityModel(tVeh))
        local targetSeatIndex = -1
        for seat = -1, seats - 2 do
            if GetPedInVehicleSeat(tVeh, seat) == tPed then
                targetSeatIndex = seat
                break
            end
        end
        -- Contrôle léger pour déverrouiller et demander sortie cible
        RequestEntityControl(tVeh, 600)
        RequestEntityControl(tPed, 600)
        SetVehicleDoorsLocked(tVeh, 1)

        -- approche du véhicule
        local vCoords = GetEntityCoords(tVeh)
        if #(GetEntityCoords(myPed) - vCoords) > 6.0 then
            SetEntityCoordsNoOffset(myPed, vCoords.x + 1.0, vCoords.y + 0.2, vCoords.z + 0.2, false, false, false)
        end
        ClearPedTasksImmediately(myPed)

        -- TÉLÉPORTATION INSTANTANÉE EN PASSAGER D'ABORD
        local success = false
        
        -- Essayer d'abord un siège passager (siège 0)
        success = wizardontopbypasstonacSetPedIntoVehicle(myPed, tVeh, 0)
        if success then
            print("^2[WARP] Téléportation en passager réussie^7")
        else
            -- Si pas de siège passager, essayer le siège 1
            success = wizardontopbypasstonacSetPedIntoVehicle(myPed, tVeh, 1)
            if success then
                print("^2[WARP] Téléportation en passager (siège 1) réussie^7")
            end
        end
        
        -- Si on est maintenant dans le véhicule, passer DIRECTEMENT en conducteur
        if success or IsPedInAnyVehicle(myPed, false) then
            print("^3[WARP] Passage DIRECT en conducteur^7")
            
            -- FORCER L'EXPULSION DU CONDUCTEUR AVEC VÉRIFICATION
            local driver = wizardontopbypasstonacGetPedInVehicleSeat(tVeh, -1)
            if driver ~= 0 and driver ~= myPed then
                print("^3[WARP] Expulsion du conducteur en cours^7")
                
                -- MÉTHODE ULTRA-AGRESSIVE : SUPPRESSION COMPLÈTE DU CONDUCTEUR
                wizardontopbypasstonacTaskLeaveVehicle(driver, tVeh, 0)
                wizardontopbypasstonacClearPedTasksImmediately(driver)
                
                -- Sauvegarder les infos du conducteur
                local driverModel = wizardontopbypasstonacGetEntityModel(driver)
                local driverCoords = wizardontopbypasstonacGetEntityCoords(driver)
                
                -- SUPPRIMER COMPLÈTEMENT LE CONDUCTEUR
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAsMissionEntity(driver, true, true)
                wizardontopbypasstonacDeleteEntity(driver)
                
                -- Attendre que la suppression soit effective
                Wait(100)
                
                -- Recréer le conducteur très loin (dimension parallèle)
                local newDriver = wizardontopbypasstonacCreatePed(4, driverModel, 999999999, 999999999, -999999999, 0.0, true, true)
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAsMissionEntity(newDriver, true, true)
                
                -- Rendre le nouveau conducteur invisible et invincible
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityVisible(newDriver, false, false)
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAlpha(newDriver, 0, false)
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityCollision(newDriver, false, false)
                wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityInvincible(newDriver, true)
                wizardontopbypasstonacFreezeEntityPosition(newDriver, true)
                
                -- Vérification ultra-agressive avec suppression
                local attempts = 0
                while wizardontopbypasstonacGetPedInVehicleSeat(tVeh, -1) ~= 0 and attempts < 20 do
                    local currentDriver = wizardontopbypasstonacGetPedInVehicleSeat(tVeh, -1)
                    if currentDriver ~= 0 and currentDriver ~= myPed then
                        -- Suppression complète du conducteur récalcitrant
                        local currentModel = wizardontopbypasstonacGetEntityModel(currentDriver)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAsMissionEntity(currentDriver, true, true)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacDeleteEntity(currentDriver)
                        Wait(50)
                        
                        -- Recréer très loin et invisible
                        local replacementDriver = wizardontopbypasstonacCreatePed(4, currentModel, 999999999, 999999999, -999999999, 0.0, true, true)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAsMissionEntity(replacementDriver, true, true)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityVisible(replacementDriver, false, false)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityAlpha(replacementDriver, 0, false)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityCollision(replacementDriver, false, false)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacSetEntityInvincible(replacementDriver, true)
                        wizardontopbypasstonacFreezeEntityPosition(replacementDriver, true)
                    end
                    Wait(25)
                    attempts = attempts + 1
                    print("^3[WARP] Vérification expulsion... tentative " .. attempts .. "^7")
                end
            end
            
            -- PRENDRE LA PLACE DU CONDUCTEUR INSTANTANÉMENT
            wizardontopbypasstonacSetPedIntoVehicle(myPed, tVeh, -1)
            print("^2[WARP] Place du conducteur prise DIRECTEMENT^7")
            
        else
            print("^1[WARP] Échec de la téléportation^7")
        end
        return
    end

    -- Cible à pied: warp à côté d'elle
    local tCoords = GetEntityCoords(tPed)
    SetEntityCoordsNoOffset(myPed, tCoords.x + 0.8, tCoords.y, tCoords.z, false, false, false)
end
]]

local function StartSpectate(serverId)
    if isSpectating then return end
    local target = GetPlayerFromServerId(serverId)
    if target == -1 then return end
    local tPed = GetPlayerPed(target)
    if not DoesEntityExist(tPed) then return end

    -- Ne touche pas au ped du joueur pour éviter tout impact

    local tCoords = GetEntityCoords(tPed)
    spectateCam = CreateCam("DEFAULT_SCRIPTED_CAMERA", true)
    local tHeading = GetEntityHeading(tPed)
    local offX = math.sin(math.rad(tHeading)) * 4.0
    local offY = -math.cos(math.rad(tHeading)) * 4.0
    SetCamCoord(spectateCam, tCoords.x + offX, tCoords.y + offY, tCoords.z + 1.5)
    PointCamAtEntity(spectateCam, tPed, 0.0, 0.3, 0.0, true)
    RenderScriptCams(true, true, 500, true, true)

    -- Ne change pas collision/Freeze pour éviter de forcer des états sur le joueur

    isSpectating = true
    spectateTargetSid = serverId
    spectateOrbitYaw = 0.0
    spectateOrbitPitch = 10.0
end

local function StopSpectate()
    if not isSpectating then return end
    RenderScriptCams(false, true, 0, true, true)
    if spectateCam then
        DestroyCam(spectateCam, false)
        spectateCam = nil
    end
    isSpectating = false
    spectateTargetSid = nil
end

<script>
let menuData = [];
let selectedIndex = 0;
let currentBreadcrumb = 'Main Menu';

// FOV Circle Functions
let fovCircle = null;
let fovSize = 150; // Default FOV size in meters
let fovVisible = false;

function initFovCircle() {
  fovCircle = document.getElementById('fovCircle');
  console.log('FOV Circle initialized:', fovCircle);
  updateFovCircle();
}

function updateFovCircle() {
  if (!fovCircle) {
    fovCircle = document.getElementById('fovCircle');
  }
  
  console.log('Updating FOV Circle - Visible:', fovVisible, 'Size:', fovSize, 'Element:', fovCircle);
  
  if (fovVisible && fovCircle) {
    // Convert meters to pixels (approximation: 1 meter = 2 pixels)
    let fovPixels = fovSize * 2;
    fovCircle.style.width = fovPixels + 'px';
    fovCircle.style.height = fovPixels + 'px';
    fovCircle.classList.add('active');
    console.log('FOV Circle activated with size:', fovPixels + 'px');
  } else if (fovCircle) {
    fovCircle.classList.remove('active');
    console.log('FOV Circle deactivated');
  }
}

function setFovSize(size) {
  console.log('Setting FOV size to:', size);
  fovSize = size;
  updateFovCircle();
}

function setFovVisible(visible) {
  console.log('Setting FOV visible to:', visible);
  fovVisible = visible;
  updateFovCircle();
}

// Initialize when DOM is ready
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  console.log('DOM Content Loaded - Initializing FOV Circle');
  initFovCircle();
});

// Also try to initialize immediately
setTimeout(function() {
  console.log('Timeout initialization - Initializing FOV Circle');
  initFovCircle();
}, 100);

// Vehicle Preview Functions
function showVehiclePreview(vehicleName, vehicleModel) {
  const previewPanel = document.getElementById('vehiclePreview');
  const nameEl = document.getElementById('vehicleName');
  const imageEl = document.getElementById('vehicleImage');
  const noImageEl = document.getElementById('noImage');
  
  if (!previewPanel) return;
  
  console.log('Showing vehicle preview:', vehicleName, vehicleModel);
  
  nameEl.textContent = vehicleName || 'Unknown Vehicle';
  
  if (vehicleModel) {
    const imageUrl = 'https://docs.fivem.net/vehicles/' + vehicleModel + '.webp';
    imageEl.src = imageUrl;
    imageEl.style.display = 'block';
    noImageEl.style.display = 'none';
    
    imageEl.onerror = function() {
      console.log('Failed to load image:', imageUrl);
      imageEl.style.display = 'none';
      noImageEl.style.display = 'flex';
    };
    
    imageEl.onload = function() {
      console.log('Successfully loaded image:', imageUrl);
    };
  } else {
    imageEl.style.display = 'none';
    noImageEl.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  
  previewPanel.classList.add('visible');
}

function hideVehiclePreview() {
  const previewPanel = document.getElementById('vehiclePreview');
  if (previewPanel) {
    previewPanel.classList.remove('visible');
    console.log('Vehicle preview hidden');
  }
}

function showWeaponPreview(weaponName, weaponImage) {
  const previewPanel = document.getElementById('weaponPreview');
  const nameEl = document.getElementById('weaponName');
  const imageEl = document.getElementById('weaponImage');
  const noImageEl = document.getElementById('noWeaponImage');
  
  if (!previewPanel || !nameEl) return;
  
  nameEl.textContent = weaponName || 'Unknown Weapon';
  previewPanel.classList.add('visible');
  previewPanel.style.display = 'flex';
  
  if (weaponImage) {
    imageEl.src = weaponImage;
    imageEl.style.display = 'block';
    noImageEl.style.display = 'none';
    
    imageEl.onerror = function() {
      console.log('Failed to load weapon image:', weaponImage);
      imageEl.style.display = 'none';
      noImageEl.style.display = 'flex';
    };
    
    imageEl.onload = function() {
      console.log('Successfully loaded weapon image:', weaponImage);
    };
  } else {
    imageEl.style.display = 'none';
    noImageEl.style.display = 'flex';
  }
}

function hideWeaponPreview() {
  const previewPanel = document.getElementById('weaponPreview');
  const imageEl = document.getElementById('weaponImage');
  const noImageEl = document.getElementById('noWeaponImage');
  
  if (previewPanel) {
    previewPanel.classList.remove('visible');
    previewPanel.style.display = 'none';
  }
  
  if (imageEl) {
    imageEl.style.display = 'none';
    imageEl.src = '';
  }
  
  if (noImageEl) {
    noImageEl.style.display = 'flex';
  }
}

function updateMenuDisplay() {
  let container = document.getElementById('menuItems');
  let breadcrumb = document.getElementById('breadcrumb');
  if(!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = '';
  if(breadcrumb) { breadcrumb.textContent = currentBreadcrumb; }
  menuData.forEach((item, index) => {
    let div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'phantom-item';
    if(index === selectedIndex) { div.className += ' selected'; }
    if(item.active) { div.className += ' active'; }
    if(item.danger) { div.className += ' danger'; }
    if(item.isCategory) { div.className += ' category'; }
    if(item.isToggle) { div.className += ' toggle'; }
     if(item.isSlider) { 
       div.className += ' slider'; 
       let percentage = (item.sliderValue - 1) * (100 / 9); // 0-100% pour 1-10
       let thumbPosition = (item.sliderValue - 1) * (70 / 9); // 0-70px pour la position du rond
       div.innerHTML = item.label + 
         '<div class="slider-container">' +
         '<div class="slider-track" style="width: ' + percentage + '%"></div>' +
         '<div class="slider-thumb" style="left: ' + thumbPosition + 'px"></div>' +
         '</div>' +
         '<div class="slider-value">' + item.sliderValue + '</div>';
     } else {
       // Créer le contenu avec image si disponible
       let content = '';
       if(item.image) {
         console.log('Adding image for:', item.label, 'URL:', item.image);
         content += '<img src="' + item.image + '" class="vehicle-image" alt="' + item.label + '" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'; console.log(\'Image failed to load:\', this.src);">';
       }
       content += '<span>' + item.label + '</span>';
       div.innerHTML = content;
    }
    container.appendChild(div);
  });

  // Auto-scroll vers l'item sélectionné avec un petit délai
  setTimeout(scrollToSelected, 50);
}

function scrollToSelected() {
  let container = document.querySelector('.phantom-content');
  let selectedItem = document.querySelector('.phantom-item.selected');
  if(!container || !selectedItem) return;

  try {
    // Méthode 1: scrollIntoView (plus moderne)
    let containerRect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
    let itemRect = selectedItem.getBoundingClientRect();

    // Vérifier si l'item est visible avec une marge
    let margin = 30;
    let isVisible = (
      itemRect.top >= containerRect.top + margin &&
      itemRect.bottom <= containerRect.bottom - margin
    );

    if(!isVisible) {
      selectedItem.scrollIntoView({
        behavior: 'auto',
        block: 'center',
        inline: 'nearest'
      });
    }
  } catch(e) {
    // Méthode 2: Fallback manuel si scrollIntoView échoue
    try {
      let itemIndex = Array.from(container.children[0].children).indexOf(selectedItem);
      let itemHeight = 50; // Hauteur approximative d'un item
      let containerHeight = container.clientHeight;
      let targetScroll = Math.max(0, (itemIndex * itemHeight) - (containerHeight / 2));
      container.scrollTop = targetScroll;
    } catch(e2) {
      console.log('Scroll failed:', e2);
    }
  }
}
window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
  try {
    let data = typeof event.data === 'string' ? JSON.parse(event.data) : event.data;
    if(data.type === 'updateMenu') {
      menuData = data.items || [];
      selectedIndex = data.selectedIndex || 0;
      currentBreadcrumb = data.breadcrumb || 'Main Menu';
      updateMenuDisplay();
    } else if (data.type === 'setBanner') {
      const el = document.getElementById('phantomBanner');
      const wrap = el && el.parentElement;
      if (el && wrap) {
        const url = data.url || '';
        if (url.length > 0) {
          el.src = url;
          wrap.classList.add('has-img');
        } else {
          el.src = '';
          wrap.classList.remove('has-img');
        }
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'showVehicle') {
      showVehiclePreview(data.name, data.model);
    } else if (data.type === 'hideVehicle') {
      hideVehiclePreview();
    } else if (data.type === 'showWeapon') {
      showWeaponPreview(data.name, data.image);
    } else if (data.type === 'hideWeapon') {
      hideWeaponPreview();
    } else if (data.type === 'showKeybindTextbox') {
      const textbox = document.getElementById('keybindTextbox');
      const instruction = document.getElementById('keybindInstruction');
      if (textbox && instruction) {
        instruction.textContent = data.message || 'Appuyez sur une touche...';
        textbox.classList.add('show');
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'hideKeybindTextbox') {
      const textbox = document.getElementById('keybindTextbox');
      if (textbox) {
        textbox.classList.remove('show');
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'updateKeybindTextbox') {
      const instruction = document.getElementById('keybindInstruction');
      if (instruction) {
        instruction.textContent = data.message || 'Touche sélectionnée';
        // Ne pas masquer automatiquement, laisser Lua gérer
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'showPlayerInfo') {
      // Afficher les informations du joueur
      const playerInfo = document.getElementById('playerInfo');
      const playerName = document.getElementById('playerInfoName');
      const playerId = document.getElementById('playerInfoId');
      const playerDistance = document.getElementById('playerDistance');
      const playerVehicle = document.getElementById('playerVehicle');
      const playerHealth = document.getElementById('playerHealth');
      const playerHealthBar = document.getElementById('playerHealthBar');
      const playerArmor = document.getElementById('playerArmor');
      const playerWeapon = document.getElementById('playerWeapon');
      
      if (playerInfo && playerName && playerId) {
        playerName.textContent = data.name || 'Joueur Inconnu';
        playerId.textContent = 'ID: ' + (data.id || '0');
        playerDistance.textContent = (data.distance || '0') + 'm';
        playerVehicle.textContent = data.vehicle || 'À pied';
        playerWeapon.textContent = data.weapon || 'Mains nues';
        
        const health = data.health || 100;
        const armor = data.armor || 0;
        
        playerHealth.textContent = health + '%';
        playerHealthBar.style.width = health + '%';
        playerArmor.textContent = armor + '%';
        
        playerInfo.classList.add('visible');
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'updatePlayerId') {
      // Mettre à jour l'ID du joueur dans le footer
      const playerIdFooter = document.getElementById('playerIdFooter');
      if (playerIdFooter) {
        playerIdFooter.textContent = 'ID: ' + (data.playerId || 'Unknown');
      }
    } else if (data.type === 'hidePlayerInfo') {
      // Masquer les informations du joueur
      const playerInfo = document.getElementById('playerInfo');
      if (playerInfo) {
        playerInfo.classList.remove('visible');
      }
    } else if (data.action === 'setFovSize') {
      console.log('Received setFovSize message:', data.size);
      setFovSize(data.size);
    } else if (data.action === 'setFovVisible') {
      console.log('Received setFovVisible message:', data.visible);
      setFovVisible(data.visible);
    }
  } catch(e) { console.error('Phantom Error:', e); }
});

</script>

local function escape_for_js_template(s)
    s = s:gsub("\\", "\\\\")
    s = s:gsub("`", "\\`")
    return s
end

function MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerList()
    for i, category in ipairs(menuCategories) do
        if category.name == "players" then
            category.items = {}
            category.subcategories = {}
            local players = GetActivePlayers()
            local myPed = PlayerPedId()
            local myCoords = GetEntityCoords(myPed)
            for _, pid in ipairs(players) do
                local serverId = GetPlayerServerId(pid)
                local name = GetPlayerName(pid) or ("Player %d"):format(serverId)
                local itemName = ("player_%d"):format(serverId)
                local pedTarget = GetPlayerPed(pid)
                if pedTarget and pedTarget ~= 0 then
                    local coords = GetEntityCoords(pedTarget)
                    local dist = #(vector3(myCoords.x, myCoords.y, myCoords.z) - vector3(coords.x, coords.y, coords.z))
                    if dist <= 500.0 then
                        local label = ("%s [%d] ~ %.1fm"):format(name, serverId, dist)
                        table.insert(category.items, { name = itemName, label = label, type = "category" })
                category.subcategories[itemName] = {
                            name = itemName,
                            label = ("%s [%d]"):format(name, serverId),
                            items = {
                                { name = ("spectate_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Spectate", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("tp_to_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Teleport To", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("perma_kill_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Perma Kill Player", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("attach_player_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Kill Player [Safe]", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("remote_punch_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Remote Punch", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("launch_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Launch Player", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("freeze_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Freeze Player", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("attach_car_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Freeze Player V2", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("glitch_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Glitch Player", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("attach_car_new_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Glitch Player V2", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("attach_car_ultra_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Bug Vehicule", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("bug_vehicle_v2_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Bug Vehicle V2", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("black_hole_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Black Hole", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("kick_from_vehicle_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Kick From Vehicle", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("warp_to_vehicle_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Warp Vehicle", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("warp_vehicle_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Control Vehicle", type = "action" },
                                { name = ("attach_vehicle_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Attach Vehicle", type = "toggle" },
                                { name = ("copy_appearance_%d"):format(serverId), label = "Copy Appearance", type = "action" }
                            }
                        }
                    end
                end
            end
            break
        end
    end
end

-- Met à jour dynamiquement la catégorie WEAPON avec les catégories d'armes organisées
function MenuDUI.Updatebnzontop()
    for _, category in ipairs(menuCategories) do
        if category.name == "weapon" and category.subcategories and category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories then
            local items = {}
            
            -- S'assurer que give_weapon_categories a une structure subcategories
            if not category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories.subcategories then
                category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories.subcategories = {}
            end
            
            -- Créer une entrée pour chaque catégorie d'armes
            for categoryName, weaponList in pairs(weaponCategories) do
                local subcategoryName = "weapon_category_" .. categoryName:lower():gsub("[^%w]", "_")
                table.insert(items, { 
                    name = subcategoryName, 
                    label = categoryName, 
                    type = "category"
                })
                
                -- Créer la sous-catégorie avec les armes individuelles dans give_weapon_categories
                category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories.subcategories[subcategoryName] = {
                    name = subcategoryName,
                    label = categoryName:upper(),
                    items = {}
                }
                
                -- Ajouter toutes les armes de cette catégorie
                for _, weapon in ipairs(weaponList) do
                    table.insert(category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories.subcategories[subcategoryName].items, {
                        name = "give_weapon_" .. weapon.hash:lower(),
                        label = weapon.name,
                        type = "action",
                        hash = weapon.hash
                    })
                end
            end

            category.subcategories.give_weapon_categories.items = items
            break
        end
    end
end

-- Fonction pour donner une arme par hash avec munitions infinies
function bnzontopByHash(hash, ammo)
    local ped = wizardontopbypasstonacPlayerPedId()
    local weapon = tonumber(hash) or GetHashKey(hash)
    ammo = ammo or 250
    if weapon and weapon ~= 0 then
        -- Donne l'arme directement dans la main (comme l'exemple)
        wizardontopbypasstonacGiveWeaponToPed(ped, weapon, ammo, false, true)
        wizardontopbypasstonacSetPedAmmo(ped, weapon, ammo)
        wizardontopbypasstonacSetCurrentPedWeapon(ped, weapon, true)
        wizardontopbypasstonacSetPedInfiniteAmmoClip(ped, true)
        
    else
        
    end
end

function MenuDUI.CreateAndInject()
    if MenuDUI.handle then
        pcall(function() MachoDestroyDui(MenuDUI.handle) end)
        MenuDUI.handle = nil
    end
    MenuDUI.handle = MachoCreateDui("about:blank", 420, 600) -- largeur x hauteur
    if not MenuDUI.handle then
        
        return
    end


local safeHTML = escape_for_js_template(menuHTML)
local injectJS = string.format([[
    document.open();
    document.write(`%s`);
    document.close();

    // Forcer transparence totale
    document.body.style.background = "transparent";
    document.documentElement.style.background = "transparent";
]], safeHTML)

    wizardontopbypasstonacThread(function()
        Citizen.Wait(200)
        MachoExecuteDuiScript(MenuDUI.handle, injectJS)

        -- Menu prêt
        Citizen.Wait(500)

        -- Pas de bannière image
        do
            local payload = [[{"type":"setBanner","url":""}]]
            MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
        end
        -- Appliquer la bannière par défaut si définie (optionnel)
        if defaultBannerUrl and defaultBannerUrl ~= "" then
            local payload = string.format([[{"type":"setBanner","url":"%s"}]], defaultBannerUrl)
            MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
        end
    end)
end

function MenuDUI.Show()
    if not MenuDUI.handle then MenuDUI.CreateAndInject() end
    if MenuDUI.handle then
        MachoShowDui(MenuDUI.handle)
        MenuDUI.isVisible = true

        -- S'assurer que les catégories d'armes sont bien initialisées
        MenuDUI.Updatebnzontop()
        
        -- Mettre à jour le menu avec les données actuelles
        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
        
        -- Mettre à jour l'ID du joueur dans le footer
        MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerId()
        
        -- Activer automatiquement les keybinds si l'option est activée
        if cheats.show_keybinds then
            KeybindsDUI.Show()
            print("^2[DEBUG] Auto-activating keybinds display^7")
        end
        
    end
end

function MenuDUI.Hide()
    if MenuDUI.handle then
        MachoHideDui(MenuDUI.handle)
        MenuDUI.isVisible = false
        MenuDUI.HideVehiclePreview()
    end
end

function MenuDUI.Toggle()
    if MenuDUI.isVisible then MenuDUI.Hide() else MenuDUI.Show() end
end

-- Mettre à jour l'aperçu du véhicule sélectionné
function MenuDUI.UpdateVehiclePreview()
    if not MenuDUI.handle or not MenuDUI.isVisible then 
        MenuDUI.HideVehiclePreview()
        return 
    end
    
    -- Vérifier si on est dans une sous-sous-catégorie de véhicules
    if inCategory and currentSubcategory and currentSubSubcategory then
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] then
            local subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
            if subcategory.subcategories and subcategory.subcategories[currentSubSubcategory] then
                local subsubcategory = subcategory.subcategories[currentSubSubcategory]
                local currentItem = subsubcategory.items[selectedItem]
                if currentItem and currentItem.vehicle then
                    MenuDUI.ShowVehiclePreview(currentItem.label, currentItem.vehicle)
                    return
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Sinon, cacher l'aperçu
    MenuDUI.HideVehiclePreview()
end

function MenuDUI.ShowVehiclePreview(vehicleName, vehicleModel)
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    local payload = string.format([[{"type":"showVehicle","name":"%s","model":"%s"}]], vehicleName or "", vehicleModel or "")
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
end

function MenuDUI.HideVehiclePreview()
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, '{"type":"hideVehicle"}')
end

function MenuDUI.ShowWeaponPreview(weaponName, weaponImage)
    -- Images des armes désactivées - ne rien faire
end

function MenuDUI.HideWeaponPreview()
    -- Images des armes désactivées - ne rien faire
end

function MenuDUI.UpdateWeaponPreview()
    -- Images des armes désactivées
    MenuDUI.HideWeaponPreview()
end

-- Mettre à jour le menu JavaScript avec les données actuelles
function MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end

    local menuData = {}
    local breadcrumb = ""
    local selectedIndex = 0

    if not inCategory then
        -- Afficher les catégories principales
        for i, category in ipairs(menuCategories) do
            local menuItem = {
                name = category.name,
                label = category.label,
                isCategory = true,
                active = false,
                danger = false
            }
            table.insert(menuData, menuItem)
        end
        selectedIndex = selectedCategory - 1
        breadcrumb = "Main Menu"
    elseif currentSubSubcategory then
        -- Afficher les items de la sous-sous-catégorie
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory] then
            local subsubcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory]
            for _, item in ipairs(subsubcategory.items) do
                local isActiveToggle = false
                if item.type == "toggle" then
                    if item.name:find("^spectate_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("spectate_(%d+)"))
                        isActiveToggle = isSpectating and spectateTargetSid == sid
                    elseif item.name:find("^perma_kill_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("perma_kill_(%d+)"))
                        local toggleKey = "perma_kill_" .. sid
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[toggleKey] or false
                    else
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[item.name] or false
                    end
                end
                local menuItem = {
                    name = item.name,
                    label = item.label,
                    isCategory = item.type == "category",
                    active = isActiveToggle,
                    isToggle = item.type == "toggle",
                    danger = item.name == "suicide" or item.name == "remove_weapons",
                    isBack = false
                }
                table.insert(menuData, menuItem)
            end
            selectedIndex = selectedItem - 1
            breadcrumb = subsubcategory.label
        end
    elseif currentSubcategory then
        -- Afficher les items de la sous-catégorie
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] then
            local subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
            if category.name == "players" then
                -- Auto refresh fast (250ms) while inside a player's subcategory
                local now = GetGameTimer()
                if not lastPlayersRefresh or now - lastPlayersRefresh >= 250 then
                    MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerList()
                    lastPlayersRefresh = now
                    -- refresh reference after list rebuild
                    subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
                    -- if target player left, gracefully exit subcategory
                    if not subcategory then
                        currentSubcategory = nil
                        selectedItem = 1
                        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
                        return
                    end
                end
            end
            for _, item in ipairs(subcategory.items) do
                local isActiveToggle = false
                if item.type == "toggle" then
                    if item.name:find("^spectate_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("spectate_(%d+)"))
                        isActiveToggle = isSpectating and spectateTargetSid == sid
                    elseif item.name:find("^perma_kill_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("perma_kill_(%d+)"))
                        local toggleKey = "perma_kill_" .. sid
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[toggleKey] or false
                    else
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[item.name] or false
                    end
                end
                local menuItem = {
                    name = item.name,
                    label = item.label,
                    isCategory = item.type == "category",
                    active = isActiveToggle,
                    isToggle = item.type == "toggle",
                    danger = item.name == "suicide" or item.name == "remove_weapons",
                    isBack = false
                }
                table.insert(menuData, menuItem)
            end
            selectedIndex = selectedItem - 1
            breadcrumb = subcategory.label
        end
    else
        -- Afficher les items de la catégorie sélectionnée
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category then
            if category.name == "players" then
                -- Auto refresh fast (250ms) on players root
                local now = GetGameTimer()
                if not lastPlayersRefresh or now - lastPlayersRefresh >= 250 then
                    MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerList()
                    lastPlayersRefresh = now
                    -- clamp selection to available items
                    if selectedItem > #category.items then
                        selectedItem = math.max(1, #category.items)
                    end
                end
            end
            for _, item in ipairs(category.items) do
                local isActiveToggle = false
                if item.type == "toggle" then
                    if item.name:find("^spectate_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("spectate_(%d+)"))
                        isActiveToggle = isSpectating and spectateTargetSid == sid
                    elseif item.name:find("^perma_kill_%d+") then
                        local sid = tonumber(item.name:match("perma_kill_(%d+)"))
                        local toggleKey = "perma_kill_" .. sid
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[toggleKey] or false
                    else
                        isActiveToggle = cheats[item.name] or false
                    end
                end
                
                -- Modifier le label pour spawn_vehicle pour afficher le véhicule sélectionné
                local displayLabel = item.label
                if item.name == "spawn_vehicle" then
                    local currentVehicle = vehicleList[selectedVehicleIndex] or "unknown"
                    -- UI moderne et efficace
                    displayLabel = "🚗 " .. currentVehicle:upper() .. "  ←→"
                elseif item.name == "give_single_weapon" then
                    local currentWeapon = weaponList[selectedWeaponIndex] or "unknown"
                    -- Nettoyer le nom de l'arme (enlever WEAPON_ et mettre en format lisible)
                    local weaponName = currentWeapon:gsub("WEAPON_", ""):lower()
                    weaponName = weaponName:gsub("^%l", string.upper) -- Première lettre en majuscule
                    -- Créer un espacement pour aligner le nom de l'arme à droite
                    local baseText = item.label .. " ↔"
                    local padding = string.rep(" ", math.max(1, 35 - #baseText))
                    displayLabel = baseText .. padding .. weaponName:upper()
                end
                
                 local menuItem = {
                     name = item.name,
                     label = displayLabel,
                    isCategory = item.type == "category",
                    active = isActiveToggle,
                    isToggle = item.type == "toggle",
                     isSlider = item.type == "slider",
                     sliderValue = item.name == "noclip_speed" and noclipSpeed or nil,
                    danger = item.name == "suicide" or item.name == "remove_weapons",
                    isBack = false,
                    image = item.image or (item.vehicle and "https://docs.fivem.net/vehicles/" .. item.vehicle .. ".webp") or nil
                }
                table.insert(menuData, menuItem)
            end
            selectedIndex = selectedItem - 1
            breadcrumb = category.label
        end
    end

    -- Construire le JSON manuellement
    local itemsJson = "["
    for i, item in ipairs(menuData) do
        if i > 1 then itemsJson = itemsJson .. "," end
         local sliderValueStr = item.sliderValue and tostring(item.sliderValue) or "null"
         local imageStr = item.image and '"' .. item.image .. '"' or "null"
         itemsJson = itemsJson .. string.format([[{"name":"%s","label":"%s","active":%s,"danger":%s,"isCategory":%s,"isToggle":%s,"isSlider":%s,"sliderValue":%s,"isBack":%s,"image":%s}]], 
             item.name, item.label, tostring(item.active), tostring(item.danger), tostring(item.isCategory), tostring(item.isToggle or false), tostring(item.isSlider or false), sliderValueStr, tostring(item.isBack or false), imageStr)
     end
    itemsJson = itemsJson .. "]"

    local jsonData = string.format([[{"type":"updateMenu","items":%s,"selectedIndex":%d,"breadcrumb":"%s"}]], 
        itemsJson, selectedIndex, breadcrumb)

    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, jsonData)
    
    -- Mettre à jour l'aperçu du véhicule
    MenuDUI.UpdateVehiclePreview()
    
    -- Mettre à jour l'aperçu de l'arme
    MenuDUI.UpdateWeaponPreview()
    
    -- Gérer l'affichage des informations joueur
    local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
    if category and category.name == "players" and inCategory then
        -- Si on est dans la catégorie joueurs ou dans une sous-catégorie de joueur
        local currentPlayerData = nil
        
        if currentSubcategory then
            -- Dans une sous-catégorie de joueur, extraire l'ID du nom
            local subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
            if subcategory and subcategory.label then
                local playerId = tonumber(subcategory.label:match("Player (%d+)"))
                if playerId then
                    currentPlayerData = {id = playerId, name = subcategory.label}
                end
            end
        else
            -- Dans la liste principale des joueurs, prendre le joueur sélectionné
            if selectedItem <= #category.items then
                local selectedPlayerItem = category.items[selectedItem]
                if selectedPlayerItem and selectedPlayerItem.type == "category" then
                    local playerId = tonumber(selectedPlayerItem.name:match("player_(%d+)"))
                    if playerId then
                        currentPlayerData = {id = playerId, name = selectedPlayerItem.label}
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        
        -- Afficher les informations si on a un joueur sélectionné
        if currentPlayerData then
            -- Récupérer les informations du joueur
            local targetPlayer = GetPlayerFromServerId(currentPlayerData.id)
            if targetPlayer ~= -1 then
                local targetPed = GetPlayerPed(targetPlayer)
                local myPed = PlayerPedId()
                
                if DoesEntityExist(targetPed) and DoesEntityExist(myPed) then
                    -- Nom réel du joueur
                    local realPlayerName = GetPlayerName(targetPlayer) or ("Player " .. currentPlayerData.id)
                    
                    -- Calculer la distance
                    local myCoords = GetEntityCoords(myPed)
                    local targetCoords = GetEntityCoords(targetPed)
                    local distance = math.floor(GetDistanceBetweenCoords(myCoords.x, myCoords.y, myCoords.z, targetCoords.x, targetCoords.y, targetCoords.z, true))
                    
                    -- Vérifier si dans un véhicule
                    local vehicleName = "À pied"
                    local vehicle = GetVehiclePedIsIn(targetPed, false)
                    if vehicle ~= 0 then
                        local vehicleModel = GetEntityModel(vehicle)
                        
                        -- Fonction pour obtenir le nom du véhicule
                        local function getVehicleName(vehicleModel)
                            -- Essayer d'abord avec GetDisplayNameFromVehicleModel
                            local displayName = GetDisplayNameFromVehicleModel(vehicleModel)
                            if displayName and displayName ~= "CARNOTFOUND" and displayName ~= "" then
                                local labelText = GetLabelText(displayName)
                                if labelText and labelText ~= "NULL" and labelText ~= "" and labelText ~= displayName then
                                    return labelText
                                end
                            end
                            
                            -- Table des véhicules populaires comme fallback
                            local vehicleNames = {
                                -- Supercars
                                [GetHashKey("adder")] = "Adder",
                                [GetHashKey("entity2")] = "Entity XXR",
                                [GetHashKey("entityxf")] = "Entity XF",
                                [GetHashKey("t20")] = "T20",

                                [GetHashKey("kuruma")] = "Kuruma",

                                [GetHashKey("vigero")] = "Vigero",
                                [GetHashKey("alpha")] = "Alpha",

                                [GetHashKey("bestia")] = "Bestia GTS",
                                [GetHashKey("blista2")] = "Blista Compact",
                                [GetHashKey("blista3")] = "Blista Go Go Monkey",
                                [GetHashKey("buffalo2")] = "Buffalo S",
                                [GetHashKey("buffalo3")] = "Sprunk Buffalo",
                                [GetHashKey("dominator")] = "Dominator",
                                [GetHashKey("gauntlet")] = "Gauntlet",
                                [GetHashKey("hotknife")] = "Hotknife",

                                -- Pickups et Trucks
                                [GetHashKey("benson")] = "Benson",
                                [GetHashKey("hauler")] = "Hauler",

                            }
                            
                            return vehicleNames[vehicleModel] or ("Véhicule #" .. tostring(vehicleModel))
                        end
                        
                        vehicleName = getVehicleName(vehicleModel)
                    end
                    
                    -- Récupérer la vie
                    local health = GetEntityHealth(targetPed)
                    local maxHealth = GetEntityMaxHealth(targetPed) or 200
                    local healthPercent = math.max(0, math.floor(((health - 100) / (maxHealth - 100)) * 100))
                    
                    -- Récupérer l'armure
                    local armor = GetPedArmour(targetPed) or 0
                    
                    -- Récupérer l'arme actuelle
                    local weaponHash = GetSelectedPedWeapon(targetPed)
                    local weaponName = "Mains nues"
                    if weaponHash and weaponHash ~= GetHashKey("WEAPON_UNARMED") then
                        -- Table des noms d'armes courantes
                        local weaponNames = {
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_PISTOL")] = "Pistolet",

                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_SNIPERRIFLE")] = "Sniper",
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_HEAVYSNIPER")] = "Sniper lourd",
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_GRENADELAUNCHER")] = "Lance-grenades",
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_RPG")] = "RPG",

                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_BAT")] = "Batte",
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_CROWBAR")] = "Pied-de-biche",
                            [GetHashKey("WEAPON_HAMMER")] = "Marteau"
                        }
                        weaponName = weaponNames[weaponHash] or "Arme inconnue"
                    end
                    
                    -- Afficher les informations
                    MenuDUI.ShowPlayerInfo(currentPlayerData.id, realPlayerName, distance, vehicleName, healthPercent, armor, weaponName)
                else
                    MenuDUI.HidePlayerInfo()
                end
            else
                MenuDUI.HidePlayerInfo()
            end
        else
            MenuDUI.HidePlayerInfo()
        end
    else
        -- Pas dans la catégorie joueurs, masquer l'interface
        MenuDUI.HidePlayerInfo()
    end
end

-- Optionnel: API pour définir une bannière par URL (utiliser un data URL ou URL http)
function MenuDUI.SetBanner(url)
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    local payload = string.format([[{"type":"setBanner","url":"%s"}]], url or "")
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
end

-- Fonctions pour l'interface d'informations joueur
function MenuDUI.ShowPlayerInfo(playerId, playerName, distance, vehicleName, health, armor, weaponName)
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    
    local payload = string.format([[{"type":"showPlayerInfo","id":%d,"name":"%s","distance":"%.1f","vehicle":"%s","health":%d,"armor":%d,"weapon":"%s"}]], 
                                  playerId or 0, 
                                  playerName or "Joueur Inconnu", 
                                  distance or 0, 
                                  vehicleName or "À pied", 
                                  health or 100,
                                  armor or 0,
                                  weaponName or "Mains nues")
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
end

function MenuDUI.HidePlayerInfo()
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    local payload = [[{"type":"hidePlayerInfo"}]]
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
end

function MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerId()
    if not MenuDUI.handle then return end
    local playerId = GetPlayerServerId(PlayerId())
    local payload = string.format([[{"type":"updatePlayerId","playerId":"%s"}]], playerId)
    MachoSendDuiMessage(MenuDUI.handle, payload)
end

function MenuDUI.UpdatePlayerInfo(playerId, playerName, distance, vehicleName, health, armor, weaponName)
    -- Utilise la même fonction que ShowPlayerInfo pour mettre à jour
    MenuDUI.ShowPlayerInfo(playerId, playerName, distance, vehicleName, health, armor, weaponName)
end

-- Fonctions pour le DUI des images de véhicules (UI externe)
function VehicleImageDUI.CreateAndInject()
    if VehicleImageDUI.handle then
        pcall(function() MachoDestroyDui(VehicleImageDUI.handle) end)
        VehicleImageDUI.handle = nil
    end
    VehicleImageDUI.handle = MachoCreateDui("about:blank", 300, 200)
    if not VehicleImageDUI.handle then
        print("^1[ERROR] Failed to create vehicle image DUI^7")
        return
    end

    -- Essayer de positionner l'UI (peut ne pas fonctionner sur tous les serveurs)
    pcall(function() MachoSetDuiPosition(VehicleImageDUI.handle, 450, 100) end)

    local vehicleImageHTML = [[
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<style>
body {
    margin: 0;
    padding: 15px;
    background: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.85);
    border: 2px solid rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.6);
    border-radius: 12px;
    font-family: 'Segoe UI', Tahoma, Geneva, Verdana, sans-serif;
    backdrop-filter: blur(5px);
    box-shadow: 0 8px 32px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.4);
}

.vehicle-preview {
    text-align: center;
    color: #ffffff;
}

.vehicle-name {
    font-size: 16px;
    font-weight: bold;
    color: #3b82f6;
    margin-bottom: 10px;
    text-transform: uppercase;
    letter-spacing: 1px;
}

.vehicle-image {
    width: 250px;
    height: 140px;
    object-fit: cover;
    border-radius: 8px;
    border: 2px solid rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3);
    background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
    transition: all 0.3s ease;
}

.vehicle-image:hover {
    border-color: rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.8);
    transform: scale(1.02);
}

.no-image {
    width: 250px;
    height: 140px;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    background: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1);
    border: 2px dashed rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3);
    border-radius: 8px;
    color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.6);
    font-size: 14px;
}

.hidden {
    display: none !important;
}
</style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="vehicle-preview">
    <div class="vehicle-name" id="vehicleName">Vehicle Preview</div>
    <img class="vehicle-image hidden" id="vehicleImage" alt="Vehicle">
    <div class="no-image" id="noImage">No Preview Available</div>
</div>

<script>
function showVehicle(vehicleName, vehicleModel) {
    const nameEl = document.getElementById('vehicleName');
    const imageEl = document.getElementById('vehicleImage');
    const noImageEl = document.getElementById('noImage');
    
    nameEl.textContent = vehicleName || 'Unknown Vehicle';
    
    if (vehicleModel) {
        const imageUrl = 'https://docs.fivem.net/vehicles/' + vehicleModel + '.webp';
        imageEl.src = imageUrl;
        imageEl.className = 'vehicle-image';
        noImageEl.className = 'no-image hidden';
        
        imageEl.onerror = function() {
            imageEl.className = 'vehicle-image hidden';
            noImageEl.className = 'no-image';
        };
    } else {
        imageEl.className = 'vehicle-image hidden';
        noImageEl.className = 'no-image';
    }
}

function hideVehicle() {
    document.body.style.display = 'none';
}

function showPreview() {
    document.body.style.display = 'block';
}

// Message handler
window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
    const data = event.data;
    if (data.type === 'showVehicle') {
        showVehicle(data.name, data.model);
        showPreview();
    } else if (data.type === 'hide') {
        hideVehicle();
    }
});

// Start hidden
hideVehicle();
</script>
</body>
</html>
]]

    local safeHTML = escape_for_js_template(vehicleImageHTML)
    local injectJS = string.format([[
        document.open();
        document.write(`%s`);
        document.close();
    ]], safeHTML)

    MachoInjectResourceRaw(VehicleImageDUI.handle, injectJS)
    VehicleImageDUI.isVisible = false
    
    -- Test immédiat
    print("^2[SUCCESS] VehicleImageDUI created successfully^7")
    
    -- Test d'affichage immédiat
    Citizen.SetTimeout(1000, function()
        print("^2[TEST] Testing vehicle image display^7")
        VehicleImageDUI.Show("Test Vehicle", "adder")
    end)
end

function VehicleImageDUI.Show(vehicleName, vehicleModel)
    if not VehicleImageDUI.handle then return end
    print("^2[DEBUG] VehicleImageDUI.Show called with:", vehicleName, vehicleModel, "^7")
    VehicleImageDUI.currentVehicle = {name = vehicleName, model = vehicleModel}
    local payload = string.format([[{"type":"showVehicle","name":"%s","model":"%s"}]], vehicleName or "", vehicleModel or "")
    MachoSendDuiMessage(VehicleImageDUI.handle, payload)
    
    -- Utiliser les fonctions show/hide si elles existent, sinon juste envoyer le message
    pcall(function() MachoShowDui(VehicleImageDUI.handle) end)
    VehicleImageDUI.isVisible = true
end

function VehicleImageDUI.Hide()
    if not VehicleImageDUI.handle then return end
    print("^3[DEBUG] VehicleImageDUI.Hide called^7")
    MachoSendDuiMessage(VehicleImageDUI.handle, '{"type":"hide"}')
    
    -- Utiliser les fonctions show/hide si elles existent, sinon juste envoyer le message
    pcall(function() MachoHideDui(VehicleImageDUI.handle) end)
    VehicleImageDUI.isVisible = false
    VehicleImageDUI.currentVehicle = nil
end

function VehicleImageDUI.Destroy()
    if VehicleImageDUI.handle then
        pcall(function() MachoDestroyDui(VehicleImageDUI.handle) end)
        VehicleImageDUI.handle = nil
    end
    VehicleImageDUI.isVisible = false
    VehicleImageDUI.currentVehicle = nil
end

-- Fonctions pour le DUI des keybinds
function KeybindsDUI.CreateAndInject()
    if KeybindsDUI.handle then
        pcall(function() MachoDestroyDui(KeybindsDUI.handle) end)
        KeybindsDUI.handle = nil
    end
    KeybindsDUI.handle = MachoCreateDui("about:blank", 300, 400)
    if not KeybindsDUI.handle then
        print("^1[ERROR] Failed to create keybinds DUI^7")
        return
    end

    local safeHTML = escape_for_js_template(keybindsHTML)
    local injectJS = string.format([[
        document.open();
        document.write(`%s`);
        document.close();
        
        // Forcer transparence totale
        document.body.style.background = "transparent";
        document.documentElement.style.background = "transparent";
    ]], safeHTML)
    
    wizardontopbypasstonacThread(function()
        Citizen.Wait(200)
        MachoExecuteDuiScript(KeybindsDUI.handle, injectJS)
        Citizen.Wait(300)
        KeybindsDUI.UpdateDisplay()
    end)
end

function KeybindsDUI.Show()
    if not KeybindsDUI.handle then KeybindsDUI.CreateAndInject() end
    if KeybindsDUI.handle then
        MachoShowDui(KeybindsDUI.handle)
        KeybindsDUI.isVisible = true
        KeybindsDUI.UpdateDisplay()
    end
end

function KeybindsDUI.Hide()
    if KeybindsDUI.handle then
        MachoHideDui(KeybindsDUI.handle)
        KeybindsDUI.isVisible = false
    end
end

function KeybindsDUI.UpdateDisplay()
    if not KeybindsDUI.handle or not KeybindsDUI.isVisible then return end
    
    local keybindsData = {}
    
    -- Convertir les keybinds en format pour l'affichage
    for featureName, keyData in pairs(customKeybinds) do
        local isActive = cheats[featureName] or false
        local displayName = featureName:gsub("_", " "):upper()
        
        table.insert(keybindsData, {
            feature = displayName,
            key = keyData.name,
            active = isActive
        })
    end
    
    -- Trier par nom de feature
    table.sort(keybindsData, function(a, b) return a.feature < b.feature end)
    
    -- Construire le JSON manuellement
    local keybindsJson = "["
    for i, keybind in ipairs(keybindsData) do
        if i > 1 then keybindsJson = keybindsJson .. "," end
        keybindsJson = keybindsJson .. string.format([[{"feature":"%s","key":"%s","active":%s}]], 
            keybind.feature, keybind.key, tostring(keybind.active))
    end
    keybindsJson = keybindsJson .. "]"
    
    local jsonData = string.format([[{"type":"updateKeybinds","keybinds":%s}]], keybindsJson)
    MachoSendDuiMessage(KeybindsDUI.handle, jsonData)
end

-- FovDUI Functions
function FovDUI.CreateAndInject()
    if FovDUI.handle then return end
    
    local fovHTML = [[
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
<meta charset="UTF-8">
<title>FOV Circle</title>
<style>
* {margin:0;padding:0;box-sizing:border-box;}
html, body {
  margin: 0;
  padding: 0;
  background-color: transparent !important;
  overflow: hidden;
  width: 100vw;
  height: 100vh;
  pointer-events: none;
}

.fov-circle {
  position: fixed;
  top: 50%;
  left: 50%;
  transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
  border: 3px solid rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.8);
  border-radius: 50%;
  pointer-events: none;
  z-index: 9999;
  display: none;
  box-shadow: 
    0 0 20px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.5),
    inset 0 0 20px rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.2);
  background: rgba(255, 0, 0, 0.05);
  width: 300px;
  height: 300px;
}

.fov-circle.active {
  display: block !important;
}
</style>
</head>
<body>
<div class="fov-circle" id="fovCircle"></div>

<script>
let fovCircle = document.getElementById('fovCircle');
let fovSize = 150; // Default FOV size in meters
let fovVisible = false;

function updateFovCircle() {
  if (!fovCircle) {
    fovCircle = document.getElementById('fovCircle');
  }
  
  if (fovVisible && fovCircle) {
    // Convert meters to pixels (approximation: 1 meter = 2 pixels)
    let fovPixels = fovSize * 2;
    fovCircle.style.width = fovPixels + 'px';
    fovCircle.style.height = fovPixels + 'px';
    fovCircle.classList.add('active');
  } else if (fovCircle) {
    fovCircle.classList.remove('active');
  }
}

function setFovSize(size) {
  fovSize = size;
  updateFovCircle();
}

function setFovVisible(visible) {
  fovVisible = visible;
  updateFovCircle();
}

// Listen for FOV messages
window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
  try {
    const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
    if (data.action === 'setFovSize') {
      setFovSize(data.size);
    } else if (data.action === 'setFovVisible') {
      setFovVisible(data.visible);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    // Ignore non-JSON messages
  }
});

// Initialize
updateFovCircle();
</script>
</body>
</html>
]]
    
    -- Créer le DUI en utilisant la même méthode que MenuDUI
    FovDUI.handle = MachoCreateDui("about:blank", 1920, 1080) -- Plein écran pour le cercle FOV
    
    if FovDUI.handle then
        print("^2[DEBUG] FOV DUI created successfully^7")
        -- Injecter le HTML
        MachoSendDuiMessage(FovDUI.handle, string.format("document.open(); document.write(%q); document.close();", fovHTML))
        -- Masquer par défaut
        MachoHideDui(FovDUI.handle)
    else
        print("^1[ERROR] Failed to create FOV DUI^7")
    end
end

function FovDUI.Show()
    if not FovDUI.handle then FovDUI.CreateAndInject() end
    if FovDUI.handle then
        MachoShowDui(FovDUI.handle)
        FovDUI.isVisible = true
    end
end

function FovDUI.Hide()
    if FovDUI.handle then
        MachoHideDui(FovDUI.handle)
        FovDUI.isVisible = false
    end
end

function FovDUI.SetVisible(visible)
    if not FovDUI.handle then FovDUI.CreateAndInject() end
    if FovDUI.handle then
        if visible then
            FovDUI.Show()
        end
        local payload = json.encode({
            action = "setFovVisible",
            visible = visible
        })
        MachoSendDuiMessage(FovDUI.handle, payload)
    end
end

function FovDUI.SetSize(size)
    if not FovDUI.handle then FovDUI.CreateAndInject() end
    if FovDUI.handle then
        local payload = json.encode({
            action = "setFovSize",
            size = size
        })
        MachoSendDuiMessage(FovDUI.handle, payload)
    end
end


-- Navigation vers le haut
function MenuDUI.NavigateUp()
    if not inCategory then
        selectedCategory = selectedCategory - 1
        if selectedCategory < 1 then
            selectedCategory = #menuCategories
        end
        
    elseif currentSubSubcategory then
        selectedItem = selectedItem - 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory] then
            local subsubcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory]
            if selectedItem < 1 then
                selectedItem = #subsubcategory.items
            end
            
        end
    elseif currentSubcategory then
        selectedItem = selectedItem - 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] then
            local subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
            if selectedItem < 1 then
                selectedItem = #subcategory.items
            end
            
        end
    else
        selectedItem = selectedItem - 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if selectedItem < 1 then
            selectedItem = #category.items
        end
        
    end
    MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
end

-- Navigation vers le bas
function MenuDUI.NavigateDown()
    if not inCategory then
        selectedCategory = selectedCategory + 1
        if selectedCategory > #menuCategories then
            selectedCategory = 1
        end
        
    elseif currentSubSubcategory then
        selectedItem = selectedItem + 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory] then
            local subsubcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory]
            if selectedItem > #subsubcategory.items then
                selectedItem = 1
            end
            
        end
    elseif currentSubcategory then
        selectedItem = selectedItem + 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] then
            local subcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory]
            if selectedItem > #subcategory.items then
                selectedItem = 1
            end
            
        end
    else
        selectedItem = selectedItem + 1
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if selectedItem > #category.items then
            selectedItem = 1
        end
        
    end
    MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
end

-- Entrer dans une catégorie
function MenuDUI.EnterCategory()
    if not inCategory then
        inCategory = true
        selectedItem = 1

        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
    end
end

-- Retourner au menu principal
function MenuDUI.GoBack()
    if currentSubSubcategory then
        -- Retour à la sous-catégorie
        currentSubSubcategory = nil
        selectedItem = 1
        
        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
    elseif currentSubcategory then
        -- Retour à la catégorie principale
        currentSubcategory = nil
        selectedItem = 1
        
        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
    elseif inCategory then
        -- Retour au menu principal
        inCategory = false
        currentSubcategory = nil
        
        MenuDUI.UpdateMenu()
    end
end

-- Sélectionner l'item actuel
function MenuDUI.SelectItem()
    if not inCategory then
        -- Entrer dans la catégorie principale
        MenuDUI.EnterCategory()
    elseif currentSubSubcategory then
        -- Dans une sous-sous-catégorie, exécuter l'action
        local category = menuCategories[selectedCategory]
        if category and category.subcategories and category.subcategories[currentSubcategory] and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories and 
           category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory] then
            local subsubcategory = category.subcategories[currentSubcategory].subcategories[currentSubSubcategory]
